***сочинить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочинить.html>сочини́ть</a> (5678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинить.html>сочини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sočinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинять.html>сочиня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to write, to compose (text, music)</li>
<li>to make up (an unreal story or excuse), to invent, to fabricate, to lie</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинявший.html>сочиня́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sočinjávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинить.html>сочини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sočinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинять.html>сочиня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sočinjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочинить.html>сочини́ть</a></b>)

<li>to make up (an unreal story or excuse), to invent, to fabricate, to lie</li></ol>

***сочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочить.html>сочи́ть</a> (13162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>сок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочить.html>сочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to emit <i>(a liquid)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сочить.html>сочи́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rána vsjó ješčó <b>sočít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound is still bleeding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get a tree sap</li></ol>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочить.html>сочи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сочный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочный.html>со́чный</a> (8172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>сок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочный.html>со́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sóčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сочне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сочне́й</b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúvstvo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feeling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span>, <span class="ann-pos">abstract noun suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">συμπάθεια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sumpátheia</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочувствие.html>сочу́вствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sočúvstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочувствие.html>сочу́вствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочувствие.html>сочу́вствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сочувствие.html>сочу́вствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>compassion, sympathy</li></ol>

***сошка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шка</a> (23478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соха.html>соха́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soxá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sóška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соха.html>соха́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soxá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automobile</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> steering joint</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bipod <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mount for a weapon</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">photography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> monopod</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stand with a horizontal <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a> for installing guns</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sóška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unimportant person, nonentity, sideman
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Кровосток">Кровосток</a></span> (lyrics and music),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столярка.html>столя́рка</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ЧБ</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>мел́кие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сошка.html>со́шки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ски</a> кобзо́ном <a href = vnd.unilang:орать.html>ору́т</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dáže meĺkije <b>sóški</b> ot staméski Kobzónom orút</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Even the trivial <b>sidemen</b> cry after Kobzon from the chisel</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***соя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́я</a> (27068)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Satsuma <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">醤油</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr"><span class="Jpan" lang="ja">そい</span>, soi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> [soj] (a variant of standard Japanese <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">醤油</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr"><span class="Jpan" lang="ja">しょうゆ</span>, shōyu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from Old to Middle Japanese <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">醬油</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr"><span class="Jpan" lang="ja">しやうゆ</span>, shauyu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Chinese">Middle Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc">醬油</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ltc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsjàng-yuw</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc">醬</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bean paste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc">油</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sója</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́й</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соевый.html>со́евый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soy, soya</li>
<li>soybean</li></ol>

***спадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спадать.html>спада́ть</a> (13315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">спа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спадать.html>спада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасть.html>спасть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to abate, to subside <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to decrease or become less in strength</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to fall, to come down</li>
<li>to drop</li>
<li>to decline</li>
<li>to fall away</li>
<li>to sag</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pádatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижаться.html>понижа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ponižátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ослабевать.html>ослабева́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oslabevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убыль.html>у́быль</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">idtí na úbylʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниспадать.html>ниспада́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nispadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***спайка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спайка.html>спа́йка</a> (24570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спайка.html>спа́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спайка.html>спа́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спайка.html>спа́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спайка.html>спа́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>adhesion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">abnormal union of surface</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>joint, seal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> commissure</li></ol>

***спалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спалить.html>спали́ть</a> (3338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спалить.html>спали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn, to scorch; to singe; to destroy with fire</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спалить.html>спали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch someone doing something illegal or disallowed, to catch red-handed</li></ol>

<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
